Our catalog with **#20250412** (Catalog version **3.4.328** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **56** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **477** products of **295** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **635** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

Microsoft Security Advisory CVE-2025-26682 | .NET Denial of Service Vulnerability Microsoft is releasing this security advisory to provide information about a vulnerability in ASP.NET Core 9.0 and ASP.NET Core 8.0. > Version 11.25.0 10.04.2025 PDF Reader: Lesezeichen im Reader jetzt sofort sichtbar Beim Öffnen eines PDFs mit Lesezeichen waren diese zunächst nicht sichtbar. Man musste erst zu einem anderen Panel in der Seitenleiste wechseln und wieder zurück, um die Lesezeichen anzuzeigen. Das Problem wurde behoben, sodass die Lesezeichen nun direkt beim Öffnen sichtbar sind.

> 
> April 7th 2025 - Version 25.1.104.1961 Fixed Sensors SNMP v3 We fixed an issue for SNMP sensors that ran into error state in certain cases when you used the SNMP v3 setting for SNMP Version and when you updated to PRTG version 25.1.104.1946. The issue occurred when your devices had the same SNMP engine ID, which could happen after cloning virtual machines with preconfigured SNMP settings for SNMP v3. A possible workaround was to use different user names per switch.
